    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app',

  <span id="freeText11384395232079358883" style="display:none">Vanessa Mazur knows she's doing the right thing. She shouldn't feel bad for quitting. Being an assistant/housekeeper/fairy godmother to the top defensive end in the National Football Organization was always supposed to be temporary. She has plans and none of them include washing extra-large underwear longer than necessary.<br /><br />But when Aiden Graves shows up at her door wanting her to come back, she's beyond shocked.<br /><br />For two years, the man known as The Wall of Winnipeg couldn't find it in him to tell her good morning or congratulate her on her birthday. Now? He's asking for the unthinkable.<br /><br />What do you say to the man who is used to getting everything he wants?</span>

Popular Answered Questions

<div id='communityQuestionsWithAnswers'>
<div class='communityQuestionAndAnswer'>
<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/1013637-i-wish-there-was-more-insight-on-aiden">I wish there was more insight on Aiden. Like when did he fall for her ? I knew he always had feelings for her but when did he realise he loved her? God at least epilogue should have been from his POV.</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_1013637'><a id="like_count_community_question_1013637" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/1013637?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">57 likes</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F29367958-the-wall-of-winnipeg-and-me">like</a></span>

</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionTimestamp'>
<a href="/questions/1013637-i-wish-there-was-more-insight-on-aiden">3 years ago</a>
</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionPermalink'>
<a href="/questions/1013637-i-wish-there-was-more-insight-on-aiden">See all 5 answers</a>
</li>
</ul>
</div>

</div>
<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/49756819-charlie-reina"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1480311912i/49756819._UX100_CR0,34,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/49756819-charlie-reina">Charlie Reina</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I agree! Even though they repeatedly say that he didn’t care about her before, at the end I still expected him to admit that he has always loved her. <a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I agree! Even though they repeatedly say that he didn’t care about her before, at the end I still expected him to admit that he has always loved her. And I kept grasping at hints that this was true. For example:<br />	* He would have fired his agent before firing her. Four times!<br />	* He’s a tyrant probably to test her and to keep her at a distance, while still keeping her close.<br />	* He knows she is secretly flipping him off...because he knows her minute expressions as much as she knows his!<br />	* He doesn’t react when she tells him she’s leaving, except—he’s grumpier than ever! Because he doesn’t want her to go.<br />	* He does notice the tiny things she does for him that’s why he throws a tantrum when she doesn’t leave his favorite peppermint on his clean sheets as usual.<br />	* He glowers and tells her, “You can go now” when he sees the creep Christian talking to her because... He's jealous!<br />	* He doesn’t defend her when his agent calls her a dinner roll because he’s not going to admit that he jerks off to fantasies about her.<br />	* He makes an effort to find her and uses any excuse to bring her back into his life. Because he can live without an assistant (obviously), but he can’t live without her.<br /><br />Of course he doesn’t realize these things and while I liked these hints (all part of the slow burn), I still expected him to admit some things at the end. Not an extended monologue because that’s not his style. But something. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1570041530" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1533461299698540893"><b>***ONE OF MY TOP FAVORITE BOOKS OF ALL TIME***</b><br/><br/>So many re-reads, it's not even funny...<br/><br/><u>REVIEW:</u><br/><br/><b>5 "I Would Lick the Sweat Off Aiden's B@lls All Day, Every Day" Stars</b><br/><br/>After reading 2014's <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20613920.Under_Locke' title='Under Locke by Mariana Zapata' rel='nofollow noopener'>Under Locke</a> and 2015's <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24044596.Kulti' title='Kulti by Mariana Zapata' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kulti</a>, I knew I enjoyed Mariana Zapata's shit. <br/><br/>But after reading this one I am officially so fucking #TeamZapata #TeamAiden #TeamMuscledHunkofSexyManMeat #RidiculousInstagram-likeParagraphofIdioticHastags that I'm going to make up <i>my</i> own nationally organized sport league (cause you know NFL...</span>
  <span id="freeText1533461299698540893" style="display:none"><b>***ONE OF MY TOP FAVORITE BOOKS OF ALL TIME***</b><br><br>So many re-reads, it's not even funny...<br><br><u>REVIEW:</u><br><br><b>5 "I Would Lick the Sweat Off Aiden's B@lls All Day, Every Day" Stars</b><br><br>After reading 2014's <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20613920.Under_Locke" title="Under Locke by Mariana Zapata" rel="nofollow noopener">Under Locke</a> and 2015's <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24044596.Kulti" title="Kulti by Mariana Zapata" rel="nofollow noopener">Kulti</a>, I knew I enjoyed Mariana Zapata's shit. <br><br>But after reading this one I am officially so fucking #TeamZapata #TeamAiden #TeamMuscledHunkofSexyManMeat #RidiculousInstagram-likeParagraphofIdioticHastags that I'm going to make up <i>my</i> own nationally organized sport league (cause you know NFL...NFO...who <i>even</i> cares) activity I shall hereafter refer to as...<br><br>...drum roll please...<br><br><b>STEALTH CHASE</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457237327ra/18337024.gif" width="500" height="213" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Or perhaps...</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457237327ra/18337025.gif" width="500" height="232" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457237327ra/18337026.gif" width="500" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>But we don't let felonies get us down here at the Stealth Chase Organization.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457237327ra/18337027.gif" width="500" height="283" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And at least in prison we could have unlimited Zapata reading time. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457237327ra/18337028.gif" width="415" height="289" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anyprisonrape, if you aren't familiar with Zapata's work, bear this in mind:<br><br>***Pay attentions smut scalers***<br><br>Zapata's books are <i>very</i> slow burn. In fact, some might consider them plain slow moving as a whole, especially considering the smexy times are always a looooong time coming (haha! pun!). <br><br>Now this is usually a HUGE problem for me.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457239242ra/18337220.gif" width="451.2" height="234.4" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have no shame in my game, so I will plainly state:<br><br>1) As I get older, I seem to have the attention span of a fruit fly. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457239242ra/18337221.gif" width="250" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I swear I'm like Benjamin Fucking Button, maturity-wise. I get more childish the older I get. Life's too short. So slower reads are not usually my bag. <br><br>2) I get blue balls in my girls parts like a priest at a Playboy party if I don't get any smexy times by the 50% mark. <br><br>Which makes me, well, cue tantrum. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457239940ra/18337290.gif" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But with Zapata - <i>especially</i> in this one - the trade-off is SO worth it. <br><br>The richness of this story is so hard to explain and the time she takes to build the relationship between Aiden and Vanessa makes it so beautiful. <br><br><b>Also, even though the pace of the story <i>is</i> slow, it doesn't <i>feel</i> slow. Something about the way Zapata writes makes it <i>seem</i> like really big stuff is happeneing during really small moments - because it <i>is</i>.</b> <br><br>I remember reading a scene where Aiden is holding Vanessa in his lap and the way Zapata wrote about how his arms hung over her thighs and his hands wrapped around her knees had me fucking enthralled. <b>Honestly, I found that scene (and other scenes in this book) more sensual than 90% of the sex scenes I've read. </b> And you know I've read a-fucking-LOT of those. <br><br>Something I also love about Zapata's writing style (which others might not) is that she only gives the h's POV. We never get Aiden's POV. <br><br>And I dig it. <br><br>It made him so enigmatic and interesting that it made this story even richer for me in much the same way that the details and the pacing does. You have to <i>read</i> to get to know the characters. You have to <i>read</i> to get to the love story. It's not handed to you within 50 pages, there is no insta-ANYTHING. <br><br>It's almost like you have to earn it in Zapata's books. And, like anything in life, the things you earn are the things you appreciate the most. And you seriously appreciate this love story by the time you get to end. <br><br>I adored this book and I adore Zapata's writing style. <i>Everything</i> is shown to you. Not told. And to me that's the sign of a truly talented author. She has easily become one of my top authors and I will forever hereafter be the front runner in the Stealth Chase games to stalk her whenever she releases anything new. <br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/SteamyReadsBlog/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1490118337i/22283577.png" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on facebook" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.instagram.com/steamyreads/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1490118337i/22283578.png" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on instagram" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://steamyreads.net/youtube/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1490120705i/22283756.png" width="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.steamyreads.net" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1490118159i/22283551._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX<br><br>DUDE!<br><br>I have seen this bad boy ALL over my newsfeed. But because of the kinda wackadoo title, I didn't pay much attention. Until I finally clicked on it to see what all the fuss was about and realized...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457175281i/18327550._SY540_.jpg" width="552" height="589" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Because it's by the awesome Mariana Zapata. And sounds fucking awesome. <br><br>WTF was I thinking not grabbing this sooner?!?!?! <br><br>Lesson here:<br><br>My GR friends are smart. <br>Listen to my GR friends.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1564848567?book_show_action=true">Jun 07, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2018-audio">2018-audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2017-audio">2017-audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2017-five-stars">2017-five-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2020-audio">2020-audio</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1564848567" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12270218904255569842"><b>5 'Team Graves' Stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%2010/19029712_10103880525063538_8564933586234311876_n_zps6d2eoe9y.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1497259125i/23004709._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 19029712_10103880525063538_8564933586234311876_n_zps6d2eoe9y.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>The Wall of Winnipeg and Me</i> was a seriously addictive slow burn romance. Once I started the audio, I couldn’t stop listening. It was over 16 hours long, but I finished it within 48 hours. There was nothing about this book I didn’t love! <br/><br/>Vanessa Mazur has worked for pro football player, Aiden Graves for 2 years. Aides is quiet, curt, and drives Vanessa crazy. She’s his assistant, but she wants more than that. So, she decides to quit and follow her real passion. Aides is </span>
  <span id="freeText12270218904255569842" style="display:none"><b>5 'Team Graves' Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%2010/19029712_10103880525063538_8564933586234311876_n_zps6d2eoe9y.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1497259125i/23004709._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 19029712_10103880525063538_8564933586234311876_n_zps6d2eoe9y.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>The Wall of Winnipeg and Me</i> was a seriously addictive slow burn romance. Once I started the audio, I couldn’t stop listening. It was over 16 hours long, but I finished it within 48 hours. There was nothing about this book I didn’t love! <br><br>Vanessa Mazur has worked for pro football player, Aiden Graves for 2 years. Aides is quiet, curt, and drives Vanessa crazy. She’s his assistant, but she wants more than that. So, she decides to quit and follow her real passion. Aides is a bit lost without Vanessa. When he shows up at her door weeks after she quit, Vanessa is in shock. But that shock becomes even more shocking when she finds out the favor he needs. Vanessa is torn. Help Aiden, or not… He didn’t treat her the best when they worked together, but the stakes are high for her here…. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“I would have done just about anything for you back then, even when you got on my nerves. I might have just waited until the last minute to push you out of oncoming traffic, but I’d still push you out of the way.” </blockquote>
</i> <br>As I said before, the story is a slow burn romance, but the pace is fast. The story between Aiden and Vanessa had such a great and natural flow. I loved watching them turn into friends, trusted confidants, and so much more. This book was seriously perfect. Aiden is the strong and silent type. He’s not close to anyone, really, but he slowly lets Vanessa in. <br><br>There were a few moments between them that left the biggest smile on my face. When Aiden showed up at a certain convention to support Vanessa, I had a perma-grin and happy tears! Both of these characters were completely fantastic. I can’t even tell you who I loved more. <br><br>I feel so gushy about this book right now! I read <i>Kulti</i> over a year ago and adored it as well. It’s apparent to me that Zapata is not a one-hit wonder. I’ll definitely be auto-buying every book of hers from here on out! A for sure favorite of mine this year, <i>The Wall of Winnipeg and Me</i> is one you don’t want to miss out on!</span>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1564900613" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6970595668602778808"><b>Reread: July 13, 2020</b><br/><br/>Shit.<br/><br/>Just finished this two hours ago. <br/><br/>And you know what I've been doing since then?<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1594665501ra/29808876.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Eating crow.<br/><br/>Well not for real, <i>obviously</i>. <br/><br/>Yuck.<br/><br/>You know, <i>eating crow</i>. As in admitting I erred. Trying to be humble because I made a mistake. Screwed up. Put my foot in my mouth.<br/><br/>[By the way, the said phrase with that godawful bird is disgusting. No offence, my English speaking friends, but the equivalent phrase in my native language <i>does</i> sound slightly better (literal translation: <i>dust oneself</i></span>
  <span id="freeText6970595668602778808" style="display:none"><b>Reread: July 13, 2020</b><br><br>Shit.<br><br>Just finished this two hours ago. <br><br>And you know what I've been doing since then?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1594665501ra/29808876.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Eating crow.<br><br>Well not for real, <i>obviously</i>. <br><br>Yuck.<br><br>You know, <i>eating crow</i>. As in admitting I erred. Trying to be humble because I made a mistake. Screwed up. Put my foot in my mouth.<br><br>[By the way, the said phrase with that godawful bird is disgusting. No offence, my English speaking friends, but the equivalent phrase in my native language <i>does</i> sound slightly better (literal translation: <i>dust oneself with ashes</i>)].<br><br>Anyhow, I took this book for granted. You see, this was my first MZ book, and thinking back, I think I was intimidated by its size. Too many pages, too much internal ramblings. I didn't give this book a real chance. So I just skim-skipped the 'boring' parts. Stupid. There are <i>no</i> boring parts in this book. In my defense, I was used to different kind of writing, the one that is more story-driven instead of character-driven.<br><br>The first indication that I may have been wrong was the fact that everybody loved this book. Even my book soulmates. Still, I continued living my <s>pitiful</s> reader's life completely clueless and unaware of the awesomeness that is Maria Zapata. Stupid me.<br><br><b>Because Aiden.</b> OH. MY. GOD. <br><br>He's Archer, Remy, Sebastian Stark, Diaz, Erik “Ripper” Jacobs, Gabe Bonner, Cal Bonner, Ian North, Levi (call sign Ace), Theo, Ghost Teague, Ronan, Grayson, Axel Carillo, Paul Langdon, Jimmy, Nate Sawyer, Ben, Hector, Tanner, Lee Nightingale and Joe Callahan - <b>all wrapped up in one big, hot YUM</b>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1556198984ra/27412783.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>And because Van.</b> I have a girl crush. No, <i>seriously</i>. I love her. LOVE.<br><br>I feel like I've fallen in love. For real. I'm not just using this phrase. I really feel like I'm <i>in love</i>. With no one in particular. I just feel it.<br><br>I am so happy I was bored to death with Hands Down. Otherwise I wouldn't have read all of those reviews, you know trying to confirm my thoughts and my unpopular opinion. I wouldn't have seen how everyone was gushing how much better, how epic The Wall of Winnipeg was. I wouldn't have made myself reread it.<br><br>And you know where The Wall of Winnipeg ended up? On my Utter Perfection shelf. Only six books reside there. Only <i>6</i>. Out of 1589. That's how much I adore this book. <br><br>So let us forget my original review and rating, shall we? Consider it a lapse of judgement. After all, we all have bad days...<br><br>And yes. I <i>am</i> sure I don't like Hands Down, Dear Aron and Luna and the Lie. I'm not too fond of the heroines. And the stories <i>are</i> boring and repetitive.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1594667118ra/29808927.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*********************<br><br><b>Original review (when I was dumb and clueless): March 6, 2016</b><br><br><b>3.5 Stars</b><br><br>Okay, I have some good news and some bad news. Let's start with the good news, shall we?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457292026ra/18343685.gif" width="”400”/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The theme.</b> This is my first book by this author and I hope it won't be my last. I'm a sucker for romances where the couple starts out as friends or enemies. Combine that with a sports theme and I'm a goner. <br><br><b>The characters.</b> I really liked both the hero and the heroine. The character build up was fantastic.<br><br>VANESSA. I think she’s awesome and I like her despite her constant insecurities about everything. She has a funny personality. Funny heroines usually tend to be annoying but Vanessa is lovable and compelling. She's smart, strong and independent. <br><br>AIDEN. Gotta love assholes. You see, I have a thing for the big jerks who redeem themselves by the end of the book, especially if they are the brooding, grumpy and uncommunicative types. Aiden is a perfect combination of all of the above.<br><br><b>The story.</b> I really liked the storyline. I learned from other reviews that this would be a slow burn romance so I went into this book completely prepared. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457292026ra/18343689.gif" width="”400”/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Honestly, I'm sick and tired of insta-love. I believe that a slow build-up is what usually makes a romance good. It makes it somehow more believable and realistic. <br><br>So if you like love-at-first-sight books or books where the heroine jumps into bed with the hero seconds after meeting him, then this book is not for you.<br><br>Now... about the bad news.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457292026ra/18343692.gif" width="”400”/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The writing.</b> Don't get me wrong, this book is very well written and there were many funny parts which had me cracking up BUT there was too much repetition and internal monologue for my liking. I started off really enjoying this book but as it went on I started to lose interest and I found myself struggling. <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457298103ra/18344219.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Overall, this book was a pretty good read. It just didn't wow me like I had hoped it would. So I'm giving it a solid 3 stars.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457292026ra/18343693.gif" width="”400”/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Overall rating: 3 stars</b><br><i>Writing style:</i> 3 stars<br><i>Story:</i> 4 stars<br><i>Flow of the story:</i> 3 stars<br><i>Character development:</i> 5 stars<br><i>Hero:</i> 4 stars<br><i>Heroine:<i> 5 stars<br><i>Secondary characters:<i> 4 stars<br><i>Tone of the book:<i> 4 stars<br><i>Emotion evoking:<i> 3 stars<br><i>Originality:</i> 4 stars<br><i>Enjoyment:</i> 3 stars<br><i>Effect on me:</i> 3 stars<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510504825i/24426022._SX540_.jpg" width='400"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"></i></i></i></i></i></i></i></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="6970595668602778808" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1571245327?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=pregnant-heroines">pregnant-heroines</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1571245327" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1519518696838281669">I listened to the audiobook version of 'The Wall of Winnipeg and Me' and it was fantastic! Talk about a terrific, slow-burn romance! I was completely sucked in to this story, little by little. <br/><br/>Aiden Graves is the formidable top defensive player in the National Football Organization. His single-minded focus on the sport has made him the best. He eats, lives and breathes football, paying little mind to anything or anyone else.<br/><br/>Accordingly, he is kind of oblivious to the goings on around him that do</span>
  <span id="freeText1519518696838281669" style="display:none">I listened to the audiobook version of 'The Wall of Winnipeg and Me' and it was fantastic! Talk about a terrific, slow-burn romance! I was completely sucked in to this story, little by little. <br /><br />Aiden Graves is the formidable top defensive player in the National Football Organization. His single-minded focus on the sport has made him the best. He eats, lives and breathes football, paying little mind to anything or anyone else.<br /><br />Accordingly, he is kind of oblivious to the goings on around him that don't directly impact his game. His personal assistant, Vanessa Mazur, is one such person. Aiden relies on her heavily for everything from his meals to updating his social media accounts, yet he hardly pays her any attention. He takes her completely for granted, not even giving her the most basic forms of acknowledgment like a "hello" in the morning. To say the least, he's very curt and kind of an ass.<br /><br />After working for Aiden for two years, Vanessa has finally saved enough money to quit her job and pursue her real passion in web design. Of course, this comes as a complete surprise to Aiden who had never bothered to get to know Vanessa. He was even unaware that she had designed websites for some of his teammates, focused entirely on himself and his own career.<br /><br />When Vanessa quits her job, Aiden gets a huge wake up call. He needs her back and is willing to do just about anything to have her. After the way he treated her, this will require some groveling and humbling on his part. Let me just say that there is nothing that I love more than some good old-fashioned groveling! I live for it in my stories.<br /><br />This time around, Aiden wants to up the ante. He faces deportation if he doesn't renew his contract soon, something that he doesn't plan to let happen. All he needs to secure his citizenship is a wife -- and we all know who he has in mind.<br /><br />What starts out as a tenuous work contract between Aiden and Vanessa soon morphs into more. For his part, Aiden was pretty clueless of how cold and indifferent he had been. Once Vanessa brings it to his attention, he really works at being a better person and treating her well. Even his lack of social graces was endearing. I fell in love with Aiden right along with Vanessa. He was just impossible to resist.<br /><br />As a heroine, Vanessa was also very personable. She was easy to relate to and I connected with her right away. She was a strong heroine, while not coming across as aggressive or heartless. Her character was perfectly balanced and really rounded out Aiden's personality.<br /><br />This is a story that will grab your attention early-on and hold it for the long haul. You won't find any insta-love here. This is a very slow-burn with a well-developed storyline and characters. Nothing feels rushed or implausible. It was simply beautiful! If you haven't read this one yet, I highly recommend it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1519518696838281669" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer17547283818974845655"><b>5 "TEAM GRAVES" STARS</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>In the same vein as her hit book Kulti, Mariana Zapata delivers a SLOW BURN story of a personal assistant, Vanessa Mazur who has finally saved enough over the two years of working for the NFO’s best defenseman, Aiden “The Wall of Winnipeg” Graves to quit. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492507701ra/22522923.gif' width='430' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Throughout her two years of working for Aiden, he doesn’t even return a hello or appreciate her in slightest. To her surprise, when this man of few words shows at her doorstep asking for her to return working f</span>
  <span id="freeText17547283818974845655" style="display:none"><b>5 "TEAM GRAVES" STARS</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>In the same vein as her hit book Kulti, Mariana Zapata delivers a SLOW BURN story of a personal assistant, Vanessa Mazur who has finally saved enough over the two years of working for the NFO’s best defenseman, Aiden “The Wall of Winnipeg” Graves to quit. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492507701ra/22522923.gif" width="430" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Throughout her two years of working for Aiden, he doesn’t even return a hello or appreciate her in slightest. To her surprise, when this man of few words shows at her doorstep asking for her to return working for him and then further presents a deal to pay off her overwhelming about school loans to pose in the eyes of the law as his wife, she more than taken back. Still, the arrangement is too good to pass up especially nixing the aspect of being his personal assistant and letting her focus on her own career. Vanessa's feelings of hurt over their non relationship is sad to face.<br><br><b>
  <i>”I wished you had respected me enough to appreciate me back when it would have meant something. I liked you. I admired you, and in the course of a few days, you killed that.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392191071ra/8515619.gif" width="430" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Aiden isn’t what readers are used to encountering and he's not a man whore at all. In fact, he actually hasn’t bother with women (messy) since his high school years. He’s been one hundred percent focused on his career and ignores woman fans and really lives up to the comparison of a wall. Marrying Vanessa to him makes the most sense and this is how he woos her.<br><br><b>
  <i>” I like you as much as I like anyone.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1456926748ra/18295340.gif" width="430" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Moving into his home for the next five years while she builds her career from her computer has these two characters falling for one another, slow but believable. I loved both of their characters, Leo the puppy, Halloween, Christmas, the elevator scene and I adored the fierce way Aiden protects Vanessa and how they become a team. Vanessa’s family aspect of the storyline was well done and quite frankly she was a terrific main character that friends will surely love. Aiden’s a man of few words but just like with the book Kulti, the story comes together in the end!!<br><br><b>
  <i>”Like football and art, like anything that anyone in the world has ever wanted, love was a dream. And just like a dream, there were no assurances behind it. It didn’t grow on its own. It didn’t blossom without food to feed it. It was the greatest in its subtleties. It was the strongest in its selflessness. And it could be forever with someone who wasn’t afraid to never give up on the possibilities it presents.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492507701ra/22522922.gif" width="430" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1658484916" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer4213979837069619886">*10TH RE-READ* - 19th December 2019. I LOVE THIS BOOK!<br/><br/><br/><br/>It's 3:39am and I've just finished one of the best books I've EVER read.<br/><br/>Seriously, I'm laying in bed bawling my fucking eyes out because I'm so fucking happy and so fucking sad at the same time cause it's all over.<br/><br/>Since October I never thought I would feel this way about a book again.<br/><br/>I don't even have the right words to express my feelings because my words just won't do this beautiful story justice.<br/><br/>Van & Aiden are EVERYTHING.<br/><br/>Oh fucking hell I</span>
  <span id="freeText4213979837069619886" style="display:none">*10TH RE-READ* - 19th December 2019. I LOVE THIS BOOK!<br /><br /><br /><br />It's 3:39am and I've just finished one of the best books I've EVER read.<br /><br />Seriously, I'm laying in bed bawling my fucking eyes out because I'm so fucking happy and so fucking sad at the same time cause it's all over.<br /><br />Since October I never thought I would feel this way about a book again.<br /><br />I don't even have the right words to express my feelings because my words just won't do this beautiful story justice.<br /><br />Van &amp; Aiden are EVERYTHING.<br /><br />Oh fucking hell I can't fucking stop!!! <br /><br />And seriously what twat fucking cries during a sex scene -----&gt; THIS dick head!<br /><br />I want to say all the disgusting things I want to do to Aiden's body but I'm far too emotional but note I would ride that fuckers face reverse cowgirl style into next week.<br /><br />GOOD LORD! <br /><br />Vanessa, by far one of the BEST heroine I've ever met in my fucking life!!<br /><br />She is up there with Ruthie! I love her so hard! <br /><br />Fuck, there is so much I want to fucking say but I can't find the bloody words!!<br /><br />I normally have verbal diarrhoea when it comes to my reviews but this fucker has left me speechless.<br /><br />This story not only consumed my whole life from start to finish but also made it into my all-time favourite books list and let me tell you that's a tough list to get on.<br /><br />I laughed. I cried. I laughed some more. I cried even harder. I swooned and cried some more.<br /><br />I will miss it more than you'll ever know and I will never forget Aiden &amp; Van and their amazing and beautiful love story for aslong as life.<br /><br />This author has giving me back my love for reading and I couldn't thank her enough. <br /><br />The Wall of Winnipeg and Me &lt;3<br /><br />Here come the water works...AGAIN.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover">TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=let-me-have-your-babies">let-me-have-your-babies</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1571833101" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6002064680628260798"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458259651i/18463174._SY540_.jpg' width='450' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Five words can sum up this book for me…<br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Ovaries. Where are my ovaries?” – Vanessa</i>
</b><br/><br/>Usually, when a book is recommended to me and a lot of people seem to love it, 95% of the time I’m like the black sheep of the group, the one who doesn’t understand the hype. So I was a little reluctant to try this one out. But I am so freaking happy to say I loved this and completely get why it has been all over my Instagram and Goodreads feed and recommended multiple times.<br/><br/>I’m usually not a fan of slow burning</span>
  <span id="freeText6002064680628260798" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458259651i/18463174._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Five words can sum up this book for me…<br><br><b>
  <i>“Ovaries. Where are my ovaries?” – Vanessa</i>
</b><br><br>Usually, when a book is recommended to me and a lot of people seem to love it, 95% of the time I’m like the black sheep of the group, the one who doesn’t understand the hype. So I was a little reluctant to try this one out. But I am so freaking happy to say I loved this and completely get why it has been all over my Instagram and Goodreads feed and recommended multiple times.<br><br>I’m usually not a fan of slow burning books. Mainly because I find the ‘in between’ just full of fluff and nonsense. But not this book! As my friend/buddy-reader Cynthia said, this book is sweet torture. <b>Sweet, delicious, slow burning, torture.</b> So slow that I thought I was going to have a damn stroke by the time these two actually kissed. But it worked. It worked because everything is SHOWN to the reader, not told. (And even though there was some repetition and a lot of inner monologue that would usually annoy me, this book sucked me in so much that I just didn’t mind at all.) It worked SO WELL that even the smallest gesture or simplest line from Aiden had me weeping like a child.<br><br>I don’t want to say a word on the plot. Mainly because the “twist” in here drives the plot and I loved where it took the story and was glad I didn’t know beforehand.<br><br>Vanessa was a hysterical spitfire, and Aiden was like this huge, sometimes (<i>ok – always</i>) grumpy teddy bear you just want to hug. And hump. The character development and the build of the relationship between these two were done perfectly.<br><br>It was all just beautiful. Intense and passionate and sensual and hysterical and beautiful.<br><br>READ IT!!!!!!!!<br><br>The Wall of Winnipeg and Me is out now! | <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1McqOs2">http://amzn.to/1McqOs2</a><br><br><a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com/" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467902722i/19644381._SX540_.jpg" width="275" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    <a title="EmBibliophile" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/62566585-embibliophile"><img alt="EmBibliophile" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551380716p2/62566585.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2734098718?book_show_action=true">Sep 08, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="EmBibliophile" class="user" itemprop="url" name="EmBibliophile" href="/user/show/62566585-embibliophile">EmBibliophile</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/62566585-embibliophile?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2734098718" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16959105752308692017">Re-read #2 (6/29/2020) I’ve been wanting to re-read this book for a while and now that we are going to have Zac’s book I finally have the perfect excuse to do that! This time I tried the audiobook and it was just so good. let me tell you that a sixteen hours long audiobook is nothing and nearly not enough if you’re enjoying your time. This is still hands down my favorite Mariana Zapata’s book. Zac is such an interesting charismatic character, I’m glad that he’s getting his own book! <br/><br/><b>5 ‘Team Grav</b></span>
  <span id="freeText16959105752308692017" style="display:none">Re-read #2 (6/29/2020) I’ve been wanting to re-read this book for a while and now that we are going to have Zac’s book I finally have the perfect excuse to do that! This time I tried the audiobook and it was just so good. let me tell you that a sixteen hours long audiobook is nothing and nearly not enough if you’re enjoying your time. This is still hands down my favorite Mariana Zapata’s book. Zac is such an interesting charismatic character, I’m glad that he’s getting his own book! <br><br><b>5 ‘Team Graves’ stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1567971132i/28119572._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>This book was slower than me when I tried to run a marathon once!!<br><br>But Waw! This is definitely my favorite Mariana Zapata book ever!!! It’s so adorable! <br><br>I’m a sucker for these type of books. A perfect marriage of convenience with a slow burn romance and I mean really SLOW, but there wasn’t a single detail that was unnecessary, and not a single moment did I feel bored! I loved how you were not told the story, it was showed to you instead. You feel it and experience it, like you’re living it with them. My only complain, is that I WANTED MORE! I enjoyed this book a lot! But I really wanted/needed to see more of them together!! <br><br>This book was so adorable. I was smiling like an idiot from the beginning to the end and as much as I would like to say that I’m not an overemotional girl and can’t be flattered easily, I was feeling like Awwww throughout the whole book! This book might not be for everyone due to the slow burn which I really don’t mind in books like that, and if you don’t mind as well, you definitely need to give it a try! This book -even though it was really HUGE- got me so hooked. I couldn’t put it down.<br><br><b>Song recommendation:</b><br>The middle by Maren Morris, ft Zedd<br>Hanging by a moment by lifehouse</span>

<div id="review_2266493674" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2266493674" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2266493674?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=alphaboys">alphaboys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=2contemporary-lovestories">2contemporary-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=sports">sports</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2266493674" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18217909015753652639"><b>
  <u>A.W.E.S.O.M.E </u>
</b><br/><br/>I didn't sleep much last night, but it was worth it...<br/><br/>Aiden Graves the so-called:<br/><br/><b>The Wall of <br/>W…willful<br/>I… impressive<br/>N… not-open<br/>N… noteworthy<br/>I… irresistible<br/>P… plant-eater<br/>E… enormous<br/>G… grumpy</b><br/><br/>The “You say it best when you say nothing at all” kind of guy. I loved him!<br/><br/>Vanessa Mazur, the girl who makes most of the noise when she is thinking and overanalyzing things. I felt for her. I really did.<br/>It was not easy to be assistant/housekeeper/fairy godmother/ mother/ vegan cook/errandgirl/</span>
  <span id="freeText18217909015753652639" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>A.W.E.S.O.M.E </u>
</b><br /><br />I didn't sleep much last night, but it was worth it...<br /><br />Aiden Graves the so-called:<br /><br /><b>The Wall of <br />W…willful<br />I… impressive<br />N… not-open<br />N… noteworthy<br />I… irresistible<br />P… plant-eater<br />E… enormous<br />G… grumpy</b><br /><br />The “You say it best when you say nothing at all” kind of guy. I loved him!<br /><br />Vanessa Mazur, the girl who makes most of the noise when she is thinking and overanalyzing things. I felt for her. I really did.<br />It was not easy to be assistant/housekeeper/fairy godmother/ mother/ vegan cook/errandgirl/ photographer/social media keeper to the top defensive end in the National Football Organization. <br />Especially when he never says “Thank you”. Never. Not even when you put chocolate on his clean pillow. Or you delay your dreams only to be his servant.<br /><br />So…<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I want to thank you for everything you’ve done for me” —in hindsight, that had been pretty suck-up of me to say; he hadn’t actually done anything besides pay me, but oh well— “but I’d like for you to find someone to replace me.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />And just like that Aiden has stopped being a part of Vanny’s life. And Vanny can finally wake up late, breath freely, starts training for the marathon, does her dream job without interruptions, starts dating etc.<br /><br />And all these last for about a month, until Aiden bulldozes himself back to Vanny’s life and demands that she becomes again his assistant/housekeeper/fairy godmother/ mother/ vegan cook/errandgirl/ photographer/social media keeper.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I want you to come back.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />Of course Vanni is not very agreeable to coming back.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Are you… are you on drugs right now?”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />Thus, Aiden tries a different approach to get her back.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Marry me.”<br />“What?” It came out of my mouth as surprised and rude as I imagined it did, I was positive of it.<br />He was on drugs. He was seriously on fucking drugs.<br />“Marry me,” he repeated himself, like I hadn’t heard him the first time.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />As expected, he has an excuse for this proposal. Aiden is Canadian and he needs an American citizen to marry him in order to get his permanent residency.<br /><br />This is a really funny romantic story. Mostly in the story Vanni talks too much and thinks too hard and Aiden growls. When he will lose Vanni, he will start talking. But he will still be the silent guy with only a few friends. The guy who is absolutely focused to his football games and nothing more.<br />Vanni will manage to crack open his hardened heart, but not without some punishment first (There were times that I honestly begging her to cook something for him. He was literally starving when he lost her).<br /><br />The secondary characters and stories are also interesting and entertaining.<br /><br />This is a slow burn romance. Thus, don’t expect much admission of feelings and acting on them by the main characters until the very end. <br />Nevertheless, the book was glued in my hands until I finished it during the early morning hours without getting much sleep the previous night.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>And the smile that came over the love of my life’s face made me grin like an idiot. The honesty, openness and genuine joy in Aiden’s expression still reached this part of me that hadn’t existed before him.<br />It was my smile. Our smile. The one he saved up for moments when it was only our little team together. And it didn’t hold a trace of anything football related in it.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18217909015753652639" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3407014124" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2010453616441414816"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1595339404i/29849978._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Read #8654376</b><br/><br/>So the first time I read this book, I didn't write a review as I didn't know how to explain how much I loved this book in a short review but there is no way I'm not writing a review this time.<br/><br/><b>
  <u>Me, both the times I read this book:</u>
</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520539701ra/25183234.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>'The Wall of Winnipeg and Me'</b> is a slow burn romance novel by Mariana Zapata.<br/><br/>I'm a sucker for a nice book with the whole marriage-of-conviniance and slow burn trope so I didn't hesitate to pick this book up and lets just say...<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1594479985ra/29798551.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Aiden is a football god and</span>
  <span id="freeText2010453616441414816" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1595339404i/29849978._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Read #8654376</b><br><br>So the first time I read this book, I didn't write a review as I didn't know how to explain how much I loved this book in a short review but there is no way I'm not writing a review this time.<br><br><b>
  <u>Me, both the times I read this book:</u>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520539701ra/25183234.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>'The Wall of Winnipeg and Me'</b> is a slow burn romance novel by Mariana Zapata.<br><br>I'm a sucker for a nice book with the whole marriage-of-conviniance and slow burn trope so I didn't hesitate to pick this book up and lets just say...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1594479985ra/29798551.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Aiden is a football god and Van works for him. Throughout the course of two years that Van worked for him, Aiden is quite and curt and doesn't even acknowledge her not to mention he is obnoxiously rude to her at times and is not even apologetic about it. <br><br>When Van quits, it's no surprise that she gets no reaction from Aiden, not even a nod or a shrug, which only fuels her anger. But when Aiden shows up, and keeps showing up, at her door with an absurd offer she is perplexed, buuuuttt when he offers her a deal she can't refuse, she finally caves.<br><br><b>"Touch my wife again, and I'll break every bone in your goddamn body"</b><br><br>This book was just so adorable!! I smiled so hard the entire time at Aiden's thoughtfulness and Vanessa's quirky ways. While this book may be long, it was perfect and I don't have any complains except that <b>I wanted more!</b> There wasn't even one detail that I found unrequired and I didn't feel bored for even a moment throughout the book.<br><br><b>“That’s my girl. That’s my fucking girl.” </b><br><br>I'm honestly so gushy about this book!! <i>'The Wall of Winnipeg and Me'</i> is a book you do not wanna miss out on and I would highly recommend it!<br><br><b>“I'm starting to understand that you can always make time for the things that matter.” </b><br><br>Oh, trust me, I plan to make time for this book ever 6 months....no wait... every month <i>at least.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="2010453616441414816" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1565778148" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1565778148" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1565778148?book_show_action=true">Mar 01, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Mariana Zapata fans, sport, romance</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1565778148" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10781262116786140730"><b>4 The Best Becoming the Best Stars<br/>* * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br/>6/24/2020 4.5 Team Zapata<br/>* * * * 1/2<br/>When I saw Mariana Zapata was doing Zac's book, I knew I needed to re-read The Wall of Winnipeg and Me. This gave me the excuse as I have always had a soft spot for this book. Re-reading did something more important, though.<br/><br/>It gave me insight into More, More of the beauty and smart advice on life Zapata gives us through this story. Really strong survivor lessons and kudos to those who had so much to overcom</b></span>
  <span id="freeText10781262116786140730" style="display:none"><b>4 The Best Becoming the Best Stars<br>* * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br>6/24/2020 4.5 Team Zapata<br>* * * * 1/2<br>When I saw Mariana Zapata was doing Zac's book, I knew I needed to re-read The Wall of Winnipeg and Me. This gave me the excuse as I have always had a soft spot for this book. Re-reading did something more important, though.<br><br>It gave me insight into More, More of the beauty and smart advice on life Zapata gives us through this story. Really strong survivor lessons and kudos to those who had so much to overcome. So many in this world are not given the support and love children are supposed to have from the start. This leaves them vulnerable to not only the horrific actions by the perpetrator but puts them on a fork in the road...will they succumb to the negative, the pain or will they use these lessons of what not to do and rise like a phoenix. This story gives us this life lesson so well.<br>My rating went from 4 stars to 4 1/2 because of how Aiden and Vanessa struck me the second time around. <br><br>2016 Review @@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@<br>For those who may not be familiar with the writings of Marina Zapata...reading, the blurb could lead you to believe this was another romance book of "football player needing a pretend wife" and after 200 pages.... they admit they are in love ... the end. This book in nothing like that and this is due to the style of Zapata's writing. She never does anything easy... or glossed over.</b><br><br>This is the premise, a sort of fence to wrap around all of the other intricate parts of this tale. There is so much, it is hard to know where to start without giving you the story...<br><br>What I will do is tell you my impressions of what I felt was so important while reading this...<br><br>You have two people who would seem opposites in how they have lived...but I saw so many things which tied them together...Their determination to better themselves, the stubborn streak of not wanting to say sorry or admit error and then the never quitting... of committing fully. These two were each a force in their own right. Both held so much in...so when they finally let the other know what they are feeling and thinking ...it is all the more sweet.<br><br>Vanessa had a horrible childhood...and she somehow survived it. She spent some of it in foster care and she was so lucky to have had decent caretakers. Her foster dad gave her tools to see things more clearly... to assist in handling her temper and also comfort in showing her the way to do things is to do the best you can. These sage talks of fatherly wisdom held her together for the rest of her life. They were her mantras and got her through the roughest times. <br><br>The most impressive thing about Vanessa and how Zapata created her...was her feeling of real... of a person you could believe existed...she didn't roll over for Aiden, she held a grudge much longer than any romance character I ever met...which meant normal in real life terms. She was determined and felt pain like us. She also felt insecure about where she stood in this relationship because Aiden gave nothing away.<br><br>Aiden... how can I discuss him without mentioning how every description reminded us of his muscles having muscles. I've never been up close and personal with a professional football player...but Aiden hit the mark for me in so many ways. He was the purest... not the player. He had a schedule, a plant-based food diet and dedication which was legendary. He would seem to others stoic, non communicative and unapproachable. Beneath that fortress was a huge heart and intelligence...an understanding of what is important in life... and what isn't. It was his singular focus which was his strength but also a weakness, too.<br><br>When Aiden finally realizes the wrongs he did to Vanessa, he sincerely apologizes. His experience in positive personal relationships has caused him to be a bit backward in understanding how things should work. Yet, he makes real efforts and that is the way he endears himself to us. <br><br>There are many moments of pure joy... joy in knowing someone who you thought had no clue as to how to show affection or caring.... just did. And it is the little things which bring these feelings of overwhelming joy....just like in real life.<br><br>The other factors in this story have to do with eliminating toxic people from your life. PERIOD. They may have changed, recovered but sometimes...things have happened which cannot be forgiven...and with no understanding why things "can't be forgotten" by those who did them then it is better to walk away and be ok with it. <br><br>As I said earlier, this is not a cute quick little romance. This is a meaty, slow build-up to a true relationship between two very complex people. All of the secondary characters are there for a purpose and work perfectly to move the story along. It is not a light read. It brings up abuse, domestic, and child. It will stir up feelings for these two and sometimes frustration....but always concern and care.<br><br>Marina Zapata has talent...heart and the ability to share all of it with us...aren't we lucky. <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29367958.The_Wall_of_Winnipeg_and_Me" title="The Wall of Winnipeg and Me by Mariana Zapata" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1456774327l/29367958._SY75_.jpg" alt="The Wall of Winnipeg and Me by Mariana Zapata" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <b>The Wall of Winnipeg and Me<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1565778148">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/54216251.Hands_Down" title="Hands Down by Mariana Zapata" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1592796851l/54216251._SY75_.jpg" alt="Hands Down by Mariana Zapata" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> Hands Down<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3406488839">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a></b><br><br><b>~~~~~ Before Reading ~~~~~</b><br><i>This is why I love my friends here on goodreads...<br>I found out about</i><b> Kulti by Mariana Zapata</b><i> when reviews and updates started flooding my feed. I one clicked and fell deeply in love with this author. <br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24044596.Kulti" title="Kulti by Mariana Zapata" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1419402858l/24044596._SX50_.jpg" alt="Kulti by Mariana Zapata" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1294232304">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><br>As things happen, time went by and other books needed reading....<br>But once again, my feed has brought me the joy of alerting me to</i> <br><br><b>The Wall of Winnipeg and Me</b><br><i>Of course, one clicked and a personal side note, my mom was born in Winnipeg, so how could I not...<br><br>So excited to dig in...Thank you again to my dear pals here on goodreads...for this is what it is all about for me... sharing, chatting and loving the books we read.</i><br><br><strong>For more Reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://starangelsreviews.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img alt=" photo banner_zpsb3ab83a0.jpg" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407612151i/10746470._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs"><img alt="Amy | Foxy Blogs" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1366176904p2/9955253.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1584709671?book_show_action=true">Mar 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy | Foxy Blogs" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs">Amy | Foxy Blogs</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Amy | Foxy Blogs by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/7897872-reanell-tisdale">Reanell Tisdale</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=2016-books">2016-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=arc-or-netgalley">arc-or-netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=march-2016">march-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=patina">patina</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=5-star-2016">5-star-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1584709671" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3519970395479705219"><b>YES! Loved this one!</b><br/><br/><u>
  <b>Two things got me to read this book:</b>
</u><br/><b>1)</b> I received a tweet from my best friend Sara telling me that said she had read this book and <b>I needed to read it. </b> The last time she said that to me was for a book I had passed over because the cover didn’t catch my eye. The original cover of<i> 'The Hook Up'</i> didn’t do it for me. Luckily, she told me to read it because it became one of my favorite reads of 2014. <br/><b>2)</b> Book Babes Unite had a giveaway offering 3 of Ms. Zapata’s books. I enter</span>
  <span id="freeText3519970395479705219" style="display:none"><b>YES! Loved this one!</b><br><br><u>
  <b>Two things got me to read this book:</b>
</u><br><b>1)</b> I received a tweet from my best friend Sara telling me that said she had read this book and <b>I needed to read it. </b> The last time she said that to me was for a book I had passed over because the cover didn’t catch my eye. The original cover of<i> 'The Hook Up'</i> didn’t do it for me. Luckily, she told me to read it because it became one of my favorite reads of 2014. <br><b>2)</b> Book Babes Unite had a giveaway offering 3 of Ms. Zapata’s books. I entered and was the lucky winner. I was beyond excited to win because Reanell from BBU told me how great these books are and to expect a <b>slow burn romance</b>. <br><br>Prior to winning these books the sheer size of Ms. Zapata's books had held me back from giving them a try. I wasn't sure if I could find the time to read a book that size. I was assured that once I started the book it would go by quickly. <br><br>Reanell from BBU was right that this story delivers a slow burn romance. It’s actually a book I’m going to recommend my mom read because she enjoys romance stories as long as they aren’t filled with sex scene upon sex scene. <br><br>Even though this was a slow burn I wasn't frustrated by their relationship. A lot of times I will get frustrated and want to yell, <b>“JUST KISS THE GIRL!”</b> But the pacing of the story didn’t make me sexually frustrated at the characters. Their relationship had to grow through employee/employer <b>-to-</b> I tolerate your presence <b>-to-</b> I want to be friends. <br><br><b>
  <i>"I deserve better, asshole."</i>
</b> ~Vanessa<br><br><b>Aiden "The Wall of Winnipeg Graves</b> was a hero we don’t encounter very often in romance books. Yes, at times, he was a total jerk and aloof to those around him but at the same time, he wasn’t the type of jerk that chases skirts. He was single-minded when it came to his life and career which left him little time to form relationships with others. His uninterested presence leads to <b>Vanessa</b>, his assistant, feeling undervalued and unappreciated. Their rocky start is a major obstacle that they had to figure out before they could move forward together. <br><br>One of my favorite aspects of the story is how the slow burn didn’t affect my enjoyment of the love story. The story felt believable on how the characters came to fruition with their feelings. I was held captive from the beginning of the story to the end of it. <b>The Wall of Winnipeg and Me</b> was my first book by Ms. Zapata but it won’t be my last. <br><br><b>STANDALONE</b><br><br>I won this book and 2 others (Kulti &amp; Under Locke) from Book Babes Unite giveaway. Thank you, ladies! ♥<br><br><a href="http://foxyblogs.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442610494i/16258382._SX540_.jpg" width="400" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=friends-to-luvahs">friends-to-luvahs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=low-on-smut">low-on-smut</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=first-book-read-from-author">first-book-read-from-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=pull-your-head-out">pull-your-head-out</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=over-the-top-sweet">over-the-top-sweet</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1565083420" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18325493107815102873"><b>5 Big Guy Stars</b><br/><br/>I don’t even know where to start with this review. The tale of Vanessa and Aiden snuck up on me and for that I’m forever grateful.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>“You can’t live your life bottling everything up. You need people, even if it’s only one or two, to believe in you, and as smart as that boy is, he doesn’t understand that.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>The slowish start to this story has Vanessa working as an assistant to Aiden’s pro football playing self, a job she’s only mildly tolerating. Aiden only appears to mildly tolerat</span>
  <span id="freeText18325493107815102873" style="display:none"><b>5 Big Guy Stars</b><br><br>I don’t even know where to start with this review. The tale of Vanessa and Aiden snuck up on me and for that I’m forever grateful.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You can’t live your life bottling everything up. You need people, even if it’s only one or two, to believe in you, and as smart as that boy is, he doesn’t understand that.”</i>
</b><br><br>The slowish start to this story has Vanessa working as an assistant to Aiden’s pro football playing self, a job she’s only mildly tolerating. Aiden only appears to mildly tolerate our gal Vanessa as well so her quitting to pursue her career goals shouldn’t be a problem. <br><br><b>Right?<br>Right!</b><br><br>The quiet subtlety of this story stunned me. STUNNED ME. I’ll admit to normally needing a certain level of snarky sarcasm from the book folks I get close to. Frankly, I like it that way. Maybe the obvious humor suits my book laziness, but there you go.<br><br><b>That’s not this story.<br>That’s not this story in the best way.</b><br><br>This story wasn’t a love story at all until it just was. All of a sudden I’d been sucked into 400+ pages of a book that initially I wasn’t quite sure I’d even like, but I couldn’t get enough of.<br><br><b>
  <i>So I did the only thing I could think of that he would understand, I lowered my waving hand, placed it in front of my belly and I raised up my middle finger like I had all the other hundreds of times I’d done it in the past when I thought he wasn’t looking.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457084927ra/18316404.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“I would have done just about anything for you back then, even when you got on my nerves. I might have just waited until the last minute to push you out of oncoming traffic, but I’d still push you out of the way.”</i>
</b><br><br>This is going to sound cheesy as hell so for those of you not down with that?<br><br><b>Gird your loins!</b><br><br>At the end of this read, I actually felt a wee bit honored to have gotten to experience the slow burning love between Aiden and Van. Kind of like a creepy voyeurs with permission. And trust me, it’s slow as hell, but don’t let the lack of smut bother you. It all comes together in the end.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="18325493107815102873" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1636388227" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1636388227" />
    <a title="XxTainaxX Curvy and Nerdy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19719801-xxtainaxx-curvy-and-nerdy"><img alt="XxTainaxX Curvy and Nerdy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1569767603p2/19719801.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1636388227?book_show_action=true">May 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="XxTainaxX Curvy and Nerdy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="XxTainaxX Curvy and Nerdy" href="/user/show/19719801-xxtainaxx-curvy-and-nerdy">XxTainaxX Curvy and Nerdy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1636388227" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3235321770675224280">If you're looking for a super sexy read? Well, can't say you'll find it here. Sweet? Well... eventually. Here you will find a very slow simmer. Very slow indeed. There's a lot of monologue and internalizing coming from the heroine. I won't lie and say I loved it all, but I will say that she had an interesting voice. She can be pretty hilarious at times, too. The hero, Aidan, is kind of (or maybe a lotta bit) a douche at first but the characterization is pretty amazing because his transformation </span>
  <span id="freeText3235321770675224280" style="display:none">If you're looking for a super sexy read? Well, can't say you'll find it here. Sweet? Well... eventually. Here you will find a very slow simmer. Very slow indeed. There's a lot of monologue and internalizing coming from the heroine. I won't lie and say I loved it all, but I will say that she had an interesting voice. She can be pretty hilarious at times, too. The hero, Aidan, is kind of (or maybe a lotta bit) a douche at first but the characterization is pretty amazing because his transformation goes so subtly that you find it realistic. It takes a while for us to see his depth. The book is a little on the long side and they don't even so much as kiss until close to the end but I still found myself charmed, engaged, and quite hooked. I don't want to give away too much of the plot but I'll say that there's plenty going on to keep you interested. :) Safety: No OW/OM/Sharing. No rape. Physical abuse to the h. Not by the H. Neither are Vs. No condoms.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3235321770675224280" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8420280308304861547">There's just something about the strong, silent type that draws me in and melts my heart. Aiden is that kind of guy.
