<div id="review_3142459279" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3142459279" />
    <a title="Evgeny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9340136-evgeny"><img alt="Evgeny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1544797852p2/9340136.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3142459279?book_show_action=true">Jan 18, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Evgeny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Evgeny" href="/user/show/9340136-evgeny">Evgeny</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9340136-evgeny?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3142459279" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7927756674308911109">Vanessa Mazur was working for a well-known football (I mean the sport Americans call football) player Aiden Graves as a housekeeper/secretary/PR person. The salary was good and she desperately needed money to start her own business. Aiden was playing defense and everybody familiar with the sport knows this position requires beefy guys. <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1579400583i/28802223._SX540_.jpg' alt='Defense' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Aiden was big even compared to an average defense player. Consider his Canadian origin and you will understand his nickname The Wall of Winnipeg. His attitude was</span>
  <span id="freeText7927756674308911109" style="display:none">Vanessa Mazur was working for a well-known football (I mean the sport Americans call football) player Aiden Graves as a housekeeper/secretary/PR person. The salary was good and she desperately needed money to start her own business. Aiden was playing defense and everybody familiar with the sport knows this position requires beefy guys. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1579400583i/28802223._SX540_.jpg" alt="Defense" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Aiden was big even compared to an average defense player. Consider his Canadian origin and you will understand his nickname The Wall of Winnipeg. His attitude was somewhat typical of a big people (and elephants): nothing could disturbed him and he did not care much what others think about him - after you reach certain size and proportional strength you really do not have to. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1579400679i/28802224._SX540_.jpg" alt="Elephant" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This included his attitude toward Vanessa as well. <br><br>One day Vanessa decided she has enough money to do what she always wanted (her own business - remember?) and quit. After a coupe of months of independent life she was surprised to find Aiden on her doorstep who asked her to come back. She refused. He came back another time and was refused again. Finally he made Vanessa an offer she could not refuse. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1579400810i/28802231.jpg" alt="Offer" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>No sane person could.<br><br>People familiar with works of Mariana Zapata know she redefined slow-burn romance genre. She makes any slow-burn romance not written by her look like insta-love. So let us just call her books ultra slow-burn. This is one of the examples of this.<br><br>The main characters - Vanessa and Aiden - carry the story. They are so interesting you kind of going with the flow and just keep reading. Some of the secondary characters were good, but they did not get as much time as the heroes. You read expecting something Earth-shaking happen; it never does, but for some reason you do not care. <br><br>Story: while it took forever and then some for the relationship between Vanessa and Aiden to start moving (with the glacial speed) their efforts to conquer their own personal demons - they both came from broken families - made the story exiting and fun to follow. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1579400984i/28802240.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="Personal demons" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>In other words, at least in my case I did not want to put the book down.<br><br>So the rating is 5 stars - I honestly did not expect the book to be so good when I started reading. I would not hesitate to call it a must for any fan of slow-burn romances: drop everything and read it; it is well worth it. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7927756674308911109" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3017798316" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3017798316" />
    <a title="Samantha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10067920-samantha"><img alt="Samantha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590018789p2/10067920.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3017798316?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Samantha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Samantha" href="/user/show/10067920-samantha">Samantha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10067920-samantha?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3017798316" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8733301156987243269">Since I’ve started reading more romance, I find it’s harder to rate than other genres. 2 stars for other genres would mean I didn’t enjoy this book. Which isn’t true. I was okay reading it - I just saw a lot of flaws and felt it could do with some serious editing. <br/><br/>This book could have been shorter. So much is filler. I get it - it’s slow burn romance. But I would have been so much more engaged had there been more interactions between the characters. Even a hint at romance didn’t start until 60% </span>
  <span id="freeText8733301156987243269" style="display:none">Since I’ve started reading more romance, I find it’s harder to rate than other genres. 2 stars for other genres would mean I didn’t enjoy this book. Which isn’t true. I was okay reading it - I just saw a lot of flaws and felt it could do with some serious editing. <br /><br />This book could have been shorter. So much is filler. I get it - it’s slow burn romance. But I would have been so much more engaged had there been more interactions between the characters. Even a hint at romance didn’t start until 60% in! <br /><br />Also, although I liked Aiden by the end, he literally was a wall for most of the book. Zero emotion. ZERO. I prefer my slow burn with more banter. Also he tells her to shut up a lot which bugged me. The amount of times I had to hear how big he was as a person as well.. little much. <br /><br />Some of the backstory too with both characters’ various traumas didn’t ring true to me. That part of the story felt very two dimensional and not well written. <br /><br />Did I hate this book? No. Is it a new favorite? No. It felt like turning a Hallmark movie into a miniseries. Fine to watch in the moment but way too long and shallow to enjoy over and over - for me. <br /><br />I do plan on reading more of this author just to have some pleasant enjoyable filler around when my brain needs a break. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8733301156987243269" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1566263042" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17696962845749300595"><b>4.5 <i>The Wall of Asswipe</i> Stars!</b><br/><br/>What an amazing slow burn romance. If there's one thing that's truly apparent in this book, it's the spot-on perfect writing style of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5760202.Mariana_Zapata' title='Mariana Zapata' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mariana Zapata</a>. I loved every single one of her lines, her characters' snappy dialogues, and the humor that she incorporated. She has truly brought out all the very best elements of a sports romance to keep the readers engaged.<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29367958.The_Wall_of_Winnipeg_and_Me' title='The Wall of Winnipeg and Me by Mariana Zapata' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Wall of Winnipeg and Me</a> is a hate-to-love story between the characters <b>Vanessa Mazur</b> and the NFO Defensiv</span>
  <span id="freeText17696962845749300595" style="display:none"><b>4.5 <i>The Wall of Asswipe</i> Stars!</b><br><br>What an amazing slow burn romance. If there's one thing that's truly apparent in this book, it's the spot-on perfect writing style of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5760202.Mariana_Zapata" title="Mariana Zapata" rel="nofollow noopener">Mariana Zapata</a>. I loved every single one of her lines, her characters' snappy dialogues, and the humor that she incorporated. She has truly brought out all the very best elements of a sports romance to keep the readers engaged.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29367958.The_Wall_of_Winnipeg_and_Me" title="The Wall of Winnipeg and Me by Mariana Zapata" rel="nofollow noopener">The Wall of Winnipeg and Me</a> is a hate-to-love story between the characters <b>Vanessa Mazur</b> and the NFO Defensive Player of the Year <b>Aiden Graves</b>. Vanessa has worked for Aiden as a personal assistant for about 2 years already and within those years, she didn't exactly have a good relationship with him. Aiden is the type of man who doesn't like to talk or even give a damn about her so after she quit her job, she was surprised when he came into her house, asking her to come back and even propose to her a marriage of convenience.<br><br>I'm an avid fan of sports romance so this wasn't difficult to love. For being such a long book, I enjoyed every bit of it because there wasn't a single chapter that bored me. Both characters are also easy to love. I admired their raw honesty with each other and how the romance simmered slowly while they carefully explored their bitter past and family issues. At no point their relationship felt forced. I also loved the fact that they both started as strangers and then eventually became best of friends. Stories like this are the type that you couldn't help but be drawn to.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Life was all about choices, You chose what to make out of what you had.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I couldn't also resist the fact that Aiden is such a great hero. His character development amazed me. And the way he cared for Vanessa-- ahhh I really bought his affection! Also, can I swoon over Zac? He's such a bae and his friendship with Vanessa is goals! All in all, this book was yet another enjoyable read. It was sweet and full of depth and surprises. Definitely a must read for fans of slow burn and sports-themed romances.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“When life gives you lemons, you get to choose what ou make of them; it doesn't always have to be lemonade!”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <p>
    <a href="https://pagesofpearl.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
      <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472382775i/20186886._SX540_.jpg" alt="Pages of Pearl" width="400" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
    </a>
  </p>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464648592i/19260109.png" width="250" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2255891253" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16502847682565211185"><blockquote>
  <b>"I got you."</b>
</blockquote><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1546467652i/26850502._SX540_.jpg' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>The Wall of Winnipeg and Me</b> is a slow burn contemporary romance full of passion, friendship, humor, and tender romance. Vanessa Mazur has been a personal assistant to Aiden Graves a professional football player with a huge ego. Aiden doesn't appreciate all that Vanessa does for him and when she finally gets up enough courage to quit, he is stunned. When Aiden finds himself in a unique predicament only Vanessa can help him out. But can he convince Vanessa to give him another chanc</span>
  <span id="freeText16502847682565211185" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>"I got you."</b>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1546467652i/26850502._SX540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The Wall of Winnipeg and Me</b> is a slow burn contemporary romance full of passion, friendship, humor, and tender romance. Vanessa Mazur has been a personal assistant to Aiden Graves a professional football player with a huge ego. Aiden doesn't appreciate all that Vanessa does for him and when she finally gets up enough courage to quit, he is stunned. When Aiden finds himself in a unique predicament only Vanessa can help him out. But can he convince Vanessa to give him another chance?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466701540i/19510149._SX540_.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <b>"Aiden kissed me like...good lord, like we were having slow, intense sex. At least the kind of slow, intense sex I'd seen in porns before."</b>
</blockquote> Told in multiple POV, <b>The Wall of Winnipeg and Me</b> is an absolute must-read. Aiden and Vanessa are perfectly matched and the transformation they make from enemies, to friends, to lovers is truly remarkable. The dialogue between the two is witty and fun and the supporting characters enhance the plot greatly as they interact with Aiden and Van! Although I never considered myself a fan of a slow-burn romance, the intensity and build up between Aiden and Vanessa is smoldering hot and the way in which Ms. Zapata has crafted the text immerses you in each moment and you feel every single emotion as it unfolds. I adore every single moment spent in this world! <blockquote>
  <b>"That's my girl. That's my fucking girl."</b>
</blockquote> Overall, <b>The Wall of Winnipeg and Me</b> is an absolute must read to anyone who enjoys a well written contemporary romance with complex characters and a well-developed plot. Ms. Zapata has quickly become one of my absolute favorite authors and I look forward to reading more of her work! <br><br><b>*I am listening to the audible version of this book! <br><br>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:<br><a href="https://craziesrusbookblog.wordpress.com//" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483747845i/21645810.jpg" width="320" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450764696i/17467413.jpg" width="" height="30" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><a href="https://twitter.com/CraziesRus" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450633462i/17450183.png" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.pinterest.com/craziesrus/" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450763751i/17467332.jpg" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.facebook.com/Crazies-R-Us-Book-Blog-171506803016307/timeline/" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450633462i/17450182.png" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/110273454171852792166/posts" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451963666i/17626541.png" width="55" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450764696i/17467413.jpg" width="" height="30" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b></span>

<div id="review_1507493115" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1507493115" />
    <a title="Ivy Deluca" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7751086-ivy-deluca"><img alt="Ivy Deluca" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1573265162p2/7751086.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1507493115?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ivy Deluca" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ivy Deluca" href="/user/show/7751086-ivy-deluca">Ivy Deluca</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7751086-ivy-deluca?shelf=football-romance">football-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7751086-ivy-deluca?shelf=marriage-of-convenience">marriage-of-convenience</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7751086-ivy-deluca?shelf=slow-burn">slow-burn</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7751086-ivy-deluca?shelf=latinx-heroine-heroes">latinx-heroine-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7751086-ivy-deluca?shelf=latinx-authors">latinx-authors</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1507493115" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5645240515603068556">Edited to add Mariana's inspiration for Aiden because...damn. Thank you Mariana.<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457708424i/18392510._SY540_.jpg' width='500' height='750' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The Wall of Winnipeg, aka Aiden Graves, is the premier defensive end for the Three Hundreds, a team in the National Football Organization. Vanessa Mazur is his assistant. For two years, Vanessa has taken care of Aiden’s meals, his home, his emails and social media, everything. Until the day when she was ready to give it all up. She’d had enough. She quits to focus on her dreams and says no more. Then Aiden makes her </span>
  <span id="freeText5645240515603068556" style="display:none">Edited to add Mariana's inspiration for Aiden because...damn. Thank you Mariana.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457708424i/18392510._SY540_.jpg" width="500" height="750" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The Wall of Winnipeg, aka Aiden Graves, is the premier defensive end for the Three Hundreds, a team in the National Football Organization. Vanessa Mazur is his assistant. For two years, Vanessa has taken care of Aiden’s meals, his home, his emails and social media, everything. Until the day when she was ready to give it all up. She’d had enough. She quits to focus on her dreams and says no more. Then Aiden makes her a deal that she can’t pass up - marry him for his green card, and he’d take care of her debts. There’s so much more, but ultimately, romance happens.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434745281i/15258398.png" width="400" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Writing like a boss</b>: Mariana Zapata has impressed me with every book she’s written. Each time I think I know what I’m in for, her characters surprise and enchant me. The Wall of Winnipeg and Me is no different. Vanessa and Aiden are the polar opposite of insta-love and the journey is the centerpiece. It’s an unusual romance, in that it’s about establishing these individuals first and foremost, then building that romance slowly, surely and solidly. The way it does it is through Vanessa’s eyes, and I’ll admit - You get to really know her, and I’ve got a bit of a girlcrush on her right now.<br><br><b>I love Vanessa</b>: She is what I expect in a Zapata heroine - she’s self-reliant, self-aware, never perfect but always entertaining. First person is particularly difficult to pull off well because you have to a) connect with that narrator; and b) she has to be able to deliver a full view of the world around her. Additionally, alot of times in romances, the characters seem to exist almost in a vacuum. It’s all about the relationship and their individual lives get short shrift. So not the case here. Ms. Zapata is particularly adept at building these characters and their relationships, while maintaining a good balance between humor and drama. At no time did I feel as if I was missing something because it’s strictly from Vanessa’s POV. And her view of the Wall….mmm, mmm, mmm.<br><br><b>I wouldn’t mind being a brick in that Wall</b>: Aiden is the type of hero I’ve come to expect as well - he’s stoic, focused, physically impressive, not exactly cuddly but when his emotions shine through, it’s so easy to see why Vanessa falls in love with him. His past is revealed bit by bit, showing the man behind the Wall. I think Ms. Zapata also does an excellent job in delving into the mentality of a professional athlete. Between Aiden and her other athlete hero, Reiner Kulti, I think she’s drawn two interesting heroes that are perfect matches for their heroines.<br><br><b>Slow burn worth every single moment</b>: This story takes its time to unfold, and it’s not a quick read by any means, so be prepared to settle in and immerse yourself in their lives. The characters are solidly written, the story kept me engaged from beginning to end and it's a slow burn that gave me more satisfaction than a hundred insta-love sex scenes ever could.<br><br><b>Teeny, tiny quibbles</b>: The football, and the immigration plot point, play their parts in garnishing this story, but they're more of a garnish. The immigration bit feels like a necessary evil to put these two together, which is ok. I’ve read alot of sports-themed romances, and some are definitely stronger when it comes to the sports aspect. That said, I can’t find fault with a story that I devoured in a day and kept me up late at night, wanting to read just one more chapter.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434745281i/15258399.png" width="400" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I loved this slow burn romance so much. It gives me everything I expected and the love is well worth the wait. If you haven’t read Ms. Zapata’s romances, you really should. The only thing that makes me sad is that it’s over, and I have to wait to see what she writes next. I know I’ll be reading it, whatever it is.<br><br>For more reviews, visit<br><a href="http://afterdarkbooklovers.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453917680i/17891018.jpg" width="320" height="108" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/After-Dark-Book-Lovers/290327777811010?ref_type=bookmark" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453918230i/17891087.png" width="34" height="34" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/113109434312544905742/posts" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453918230i/17891089.png" width="34" height="34" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.instagram.com/afterdarkbooklovers/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453918230i/17891088.png" width="34" height="34" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://twitter.com/AftDarkBkLovers" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453918230i/17891086.png" width="34" height="34" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

  <b>"I'm starting to understand that you can always make time for the things that </b></blockquote></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1705765768" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1705765768" />
    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1705765768?book_show_action=true">Jul 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/30120594-the-wall-of-winnipeg-and-me">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=audio">audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1705765768" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6619291903594534878"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469538941i/19828415._SX540_.jpg' width='700' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>I couldn’t help myself…</b><br/><br/>I buy audio books for my in-between reads. I like to listen to audiobooks when I’m catching the train to work, baking or exercising (which I should do more of). Well, there was a slight problem with <i>The Wall of Winnipeg and Me</i>, it was too good. I couldn’t bring myself to stop listening. What normally would have lasted me a couple of weeks lasted me a couple of days. I was sucked into the story from the very first minute. The narrator had a voice that was easy to listen to,</span>
  <span id="freeText6619291903594534878" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469538941i/19828415._SX540_.jpg" width="700" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I couldn’t help myself…</b><br><br>I buy audio books for my in-between reads. I like to listen to audiobooks when I’m catching the train to work, baking or exercising (which I should do more of). Well, there was a slight problem with <i>The Wall of Winnipeg and Me</i>, it was too good. I couldn’t bring myself to stop listening. What normally would have lasted me a couple of weeks lasted me a couple of days. I was sucked into the story from the very first minute. The narrator had a voice that was easy to listen to, the characters were engaging and the storyline was interesting. A lot of readers refer to Ms Zapata as the Queen of the Slow Burn, which honestly I’d have to agree with. What I think makes her the Queen is her ability to distract you from missing it. I think this was the first audio where I haven’t had to hide my face while listening on the train. I wasn’t squirming, blushing or turning the volume down hoping someone wasn’t overhearing the sexy times. Oh, there were a few sniffles when harsh words were spoken or we look back into painful past experiences but more times than not it was the big grin I wore that showed what I was feeling. <br><br>Now, in regards to the story…Vanessa is a woman who has had a very hard life. Her family ABSOLUTELY SUCKS!! What makes her such a great character though is that she’s moved on from her horrible family and made a success of her life. She was the PA/Housekeeper/Servant to <i>The Big Guy</i>, Aiden. He plays football and is one of the defence players…I think (I'm not really in the know about football). Her role and job aren't great but it pays well and it gives her the opportunity to be around Aiden who she has a little crush on while also saving to start her own business. <br><br>Aiden is the most focused football player I’ve ever read about. His whole life revolves around the sport. Considering his size, surprisingly he lives a vegan lifestyle which means he has to eat a lot, a lot and a wee bit more. Aiden is definitely serious about his job and his single-minded focus means that people don’t really matter to him. He is abrupt, rude and very unemotional. Having Vanessa as his assistant makes his life easier but unfortunately, for him, he doesn’t realise her value until she’s had enough and resigns.<br><br>What follows for Vanessa and Aiden is a parting of ways for a very short time. Aiden wants her back but Vanessa is starting her own business and isn’t interested in taking on the old role. Aiden needs her for a more important role this time. A role where they will have to make vows of commitment, live together and share their lives…on paper only.<br><br>I really enjoyed the story and loved the way the characters developed. I did think that Aiden acted like a douchewaffle in the beginning but enjoyed seeing him realise that there is more to life than solely focusing on football. I really struggled with Vanessa at times. She acted like a doormat and put up with Aiden for way longer than I thought was healthy. There is this underlying feeling from the very beginning that she puts up with it all because she doesn’t know any better. My struggle was that I knew that her history made her that way, but at other times you can see her strength and courage. I just wanted her to speak her mind more often and not have to have people beg her for information, demand the truth or trick her into sharing her feelings.<br><br>Well, the slow burn was REALLY slow and I thought that maybe it might end up being non-existent. Funny thing is when we did get it (eventually) it was intense and definitely blush-worthy. I loved Aiden and Vanessa together and I'm so glad that they were able to finally let down their walls and share their feelings. The epilogue was sweet and very cute.<br><br>I’m slowly getting through the backlog of Ms Zapata’s collection and what I’ve read or listened to so far has been great. I will definitely be reading more of her stories in the future.<br><br>To buy <i>The Wall of Winnipeg and Me</i> from Amazon - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2acZqeu">http://amzn.to/2acZqeu</a><br><br><br><b>I’m an Aussie chick who loves to read and review romance, drink coffee, be a <i>Style Setter</i> and stalk David Gandy. To see more of my reviews, fashion, food and pervathons -</b><br><br><a href="http://staceyissassy.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447925695i/17069306.jpg" width="170" height="170" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/Sassyreviews" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004243.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.pinterest.com/Stacey1565/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004244.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.twitter.com/StaceyisSassy" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004245.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6619291903594534878" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

		<td>
		    <b>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('sJNd6no97ZAIEtoBykNy9sCyyQZxPNs3pvCup7ky9zVxs2Fq1Iff/Yqw2gs083gXD/PCTiEuzhZYkr+Kl7YNlw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5+kc+262+7u0AwiCoL+BnfQC5IGFjYnZGDEmknDYW1gmySB7wAzJ1jahCIheD4t8O0PvydWfnPjmUze/Xlyh+g==')})
  }

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/trivia/work/48358625-the-wall-of-winnipeg-and-me">Trivia About The Wall of Winni...</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
